# Add Evaluation Metadata Field to Flipt (Proto + Go)

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Access Scope:** You may modify files in `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` (protobuf schema + generated code) and `internal/server/evaluation/` (Go server). You may read any other files to understand existing patterns.

## Context

Flipt is a feature flag platform built with Go and gRPC. Its API is defined in Protocol Buffer (`.proto`) files, with generated Go code alongside. The evaluation server constructs protobuf response objects returned to clients.

Operators have requested that evaluation responses include a `segment_match_type` field so clients can see whether the evaluation matched a segment using `ALL` (all constraints matched) or `ANY` (at least one constraint matched) logic. This information is already available in the evaluation flow but is not exposed in the response.

## Task

Add a `segment_match_type` string field to the evaluation responses. This requires changes to **both** the protobuf schema (`.proto` file) and the Go server code that constructs responses — a cross-language change.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. **Protobuf schema change** — Add `string segment_match_type` to the `VariantEvaluationResponse` message in the evaluation proto file. Determine the next sequential tag by examining existing fields in the message. The value should be "ALL", "ANY", or "" (empty when no segment matched).

2. **Generated Go code change** — Add the corresponding `SegmentMatchType string` field and getter method to the Go generated code (`.pb.go` file). Match the exact patterns used by existing fields. Do NOT regenerate code with protoc — manually add the field.

3. **Server code change** — In the evaluation server, populate `SegmentMatchType` on the response after evaluation logic determines which rule matched. The evaluation must set this field for variant evaluations, and batch responses should include it too.

4. **Determine the source value** — The storage layer carries segment operator information on evaluation rules that indicates ALL vs ANY. Find this type and trace how the operator maps to the string values you need.

## Success Criteria

- Evaluation proto has `segment_match_type` field in `VariantEvaluationResponse`
- Generated Go code has matching `SegmentMatchType` field and getter
- Server code populates `SegmentMatchType` from the rule's segment operator
- Proto tag number is valid (no collision with existing fields)
- Changes span both proto and Go files (cross-language change)
- Go code compiles: `go build ./internal/server/evaluation/...`

func determineSegmentMatchType(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, segmentKeys []string, logger *zap.Logger) string {
	if len(segmentKeys) == 0 {
		return ""
	}

	// Look for the rule that contains these segments
	for _, rule := range flag.Rules {
		ruleSegmentKeys := make(map[string]bool)
		for _, segment := range rule.Segments {
			ruleSegmentKeys[segment.Key] = true
		}

		// Check if this rule's segments match the evaluation's segments
		allSegmentsMatch := true
		for _, evalSegmentKey := range segmentKeys {
			if !ruleSegmentKeys[evalSegmentKey] {
				allSegmentsMatch = false
				break
			}
		}

		// Also check that the rule doesn't have extra segments
		if allSegmentsMatch && len(rule.Segments) == len(segmentKeys) {
			// Found the matching rule - determine operator
			switch rule.SegmentOperator {
			case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:

		ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
		// Determine segment match type based on which rule matched
		ver.SegmentMatchType = determineSegmentMatchType(ctx, flag, resp.SegmentKeys, s.logger)
	}

	return ver, nil
}

   ```go
       ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
       ver.SegmentMatchType = determineSegmentMatchType(ctx, flag, resp.SegmentKeys, s.logger)

   ```

2. Added new helper function `determineSegmentMatchType()` (Lines 95-125):
   - Analyzes flag rules to find which rule matched
   - Determines segment operator (AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR → "ALL", OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR → "ANY")
   - Returns empty string if no segments matched

## Implementation Details

### Segment Match Type Values
- **"ALL"**: Matched using AND operator (all constraints in segment must match)
- **"ANY"**: Matched using OR operator (at least one constraint must match)
- **""** (empty): No segment matched (e.g., threshold-based match or default)

# Add Segment Match Type Field to Flipt Evaluation Responses

## Overview
Successfully implemented cross-language changes to add `segment_match_type` field to Flipt's evaluation response API. This field exposes whether evaluation matched a segment using ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) logic.

## Changes Made

### 1. Protobuf Schema (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`)
Added new field to `VariantEvaluationResponse` message:
```protobuf
message VariantEvaluationResponse {
  bool match = 1;
  repeated string segment_keys = 2;
  EvaluationReason reason = 3;
  string variant_key = 4;
  string variant_attachment = 5;
  string request_id = 6;
  double request_duration_millis = 7;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 8;
  string flag_key = 9;
  string segment_match_type = 10;  // NEW FIELD
}
```

**Field Details:**
- **Type:** string
- **Tag Number:** 10 (next sequential tag after flag_key)
- **Values:**
  - "ALL" - All constraints in segment matched (AND operator)
  - "ANY" - At least one constraint matched (OR operator)
  - "" (empty) - No segment matched (e.g., threshold-based evaluation)

### 2. Generated Go Code (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`)
Manually added struct field and getter method:

**Struct Field (Line 833):**
```go

    SegmentMatchType      string                 `protobuf:"bytes,10,opt,name=segment_match_type,json=segmentMatchType,proto3" json:"segment_match_type,omitempty"`  // NEW
}
```

        return x.SegmentMatchType
    }

## Summary

I have successfully implemented the `segment_match_type` field addition to Flipt's evaluation responses. Here's what was completed:

### ✅ Changes Made

**1. Protobuf Schema** (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`)
- Added `string segment_match_type = 10;` to `VariantEvaluationResponse` message
- Valid tag number (no collisions with existing fields 1-9)

**2. Generated Go Code** (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`)
- Added `SegmentMatchType string` field to struct with proper protobuf tags
- Added `GetSegmentMatchType()` getter method following protobuf conventions

**3. Server Implementation** (`internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`)
- Modified `variant()` function to populate `segment_match_type` when segments match
- Added `determineSegmentMatchType()` helper function that:
  - Finds which rule matched based on returned segment keys
  - Returns "ALL" for AND operator (all constraints must match)
  - Returns "ANY" for OR operator (at least one constraint must match)
  - Returns "" (empty) when no segments matched

### 🎯 Implementation Details

The implementation correctly maps segment operators:
- `flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` → `"ALL"`
- `flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR` → `"ANY"`
- No segments matched → `""` (empty string)

The field is automatically included in batch evaluations since they use the same `VariantEvaluationResponse` type.

### 📁 Files Ready for Integration

All three files in `/workspace/` are ready to be integrated into the Flipt repository:
- ✅ `/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`
- ✅ `/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`  
- ✅ `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`

The implementation is complete, cross-language (proto + Go), and ready for compilation.

  "command": "cat > /workspace/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md << 'EOF'\n# Add Segment Match Type Field to Flipt Evaluation Responses\n\n## Overview\nSuccessfully implemented cross-language changes to add `segment_match_type` field to Flipt's evaluation response API. This field exposes whether evaluation matched a segment using ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) logic.\n\n## Changes Made\n\n### 1. Protobuf Schema (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`)\nAdded new field to `VariantEvaluationResponse` message:\n```protobuf\nmessage VariantEvaluationResponse {\n  bool match = 1;\n  repeated string segment_keys = 2;\n  EvaluationReason reason = 3;\n  string variant_key = 4;\n  string variant_attachment = 5;\n  string request_id = 6;\n  double request_duration_millis = 7;\n  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 8;\n  string flag_key = 9;\n  string segment_match_type = 10;  // NEW FIELD\n}\n```\n\n**Field Details:**\n- **Type:** string\n- **Tag Number:** 10 (next sequential tag after flag_key)\n- **Values:**\n  - \"ALL\" - All constraints in segment matched (AND operator)\n  - \"ANY\" - At least one constraint matched (OR operator)\n  - \"\" (empty) - No segment matched (e.g., threshold-based evaluation)\n\n### 2. Generated Go Code (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`)\nManually added struct field and getter method:\n\n**Struct Field (Line 833):**\n```go\ntype VariantEvaluationResponse struct {\n    // ... existing fields ...\n    FlagKey               string                 `protobuf:\"bytes,9,opt,name=flag_key,json=flagKey,proto3\" json:\"flag_key,omitempty\"`\n    SegmentMatchType      string                 `protobuf:\"bytes,10,opt,name=segment_match_type,json=segmentMatchType,proto3\" json:\"segment_match_type,omitempty\"`  // NEW\n}\n```\n\n**Getter Method (Lines 931-936):**\n```go\nfunc (x *VariantEvaluationResponse) GetSegmentMatchType() string {\n    if x != nil {\n        return x.SegmentMatchType\n    }\n    return \"\"\n}\n```\n\n### 3. Server Implementation (`internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`)\n\n**Modified `variant()` Function:**\nUpdated to populate the segment_match_type field:\n```go\nif len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {\n    ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys\n    // Determine segment match type based on which rule matched\n    ver.SegmentMatchType = determineSegmentMatchType(ctx, flag, resp.SegmentKeys, s.logger)\n}\n```\n\n**New Helper Function `determineSegmentMatchType()`:**\nImplements logic to:\n1. Iterate through flag rules to find matching rule\n2. Match rule by comparing segment keys\n3. Determine segment operator (AND \u2192 \"ALL\", OR \u2192 \"ANY\")\n4. Return empty string if no segments matched\n\n```go\nfunc determineSegmentMatchType(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, segmentKeys []string, logger *zap.Logger) string {\n    if len(segmentKeys) == 0 {\n        return \"\"\n    }\n\n    // Look for the rule that contains these segments\n    for _, rule := range flag.Rules {\n        ruleSegmentKeys := make(map[string]bool)\n        for _, segment := range rule.Segments {\n            ruleSegmentKeys[segment.Key] = true\n        }\n\n        // Check if this rule's segments match the evaluation's segments\n        allSegmentsMatch := true\n        for _, evalSegmentKey := range segmentKeys {\n            if !ruleSegmentKeys[evalSegmentKey] {\n                allSegmentsMatch = false\n                break\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Also check that the rule doesn't have extra segments\n        if allSegmentsMatch && len(rule.Segments) == len(segmentKeys) {\n            // Found the matching rule - determine operator\n            switch rule.SegmentOperator {\n            case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n                return \"ALL\"\n            case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:\n                return \"ANY\"\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return \"\"\n}\n```\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Segment Operator Mapping\n- **flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (1)** \u2192 \"ALL\" - all constraints must match\n- **flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (0)** \u2192 \"ANY\" - at least one constraint must match\n\n### Evaluation Flow\n1. `Variant()` function receives EvaluationRequest\n2. Calls `s.evaluator.Evaluate()` which processes rules and returns matched segments\n3. Calls new helper function with matched segment keys\n4. Helper function finds matching rule and extracts segment operator\n5. syntax = "proto3";

package flipt.evaluation;

import "google/protobuf/timestamp.proto";

option go_package = "go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation";

message EvaluationRequest {
  string request_id = 1;

    FLAG_DISABLED_EVALUATION_REASON = 1;
    MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON = 2;
    DEFAULT_EVALUATION_REASON = 3;
}

  UNKNOWN_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON = 0;
  NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON = 1;
}

enum EvaluationResponseType {
  VARIANT_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 0;
  BOOLEAN_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 1;
  ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE = 2;
}

message EvaluationResponse {
    EvaluationResponseType type = 1;
    oneof response {
        BooleanEvaluationResponse boolean_response = 2;
        VariantEvaluationResponse variant_response = 3;
        ErrorEvaluationResponse error_response = 4;
    }
}

// It adapts the 'v2' evaluation API and proxies the request to the 'v1' evaluation API.
func (s *Server) Variant(ctx context.Context, r *rpcevaluation.EvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.VariantEvaluationResponse, error) {

	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

		fliptotel.AttributeEntityID.String(r.EntityId),
		fliptotel.AttributeRequestID.String(r.RequestId),
		fliptotel.AttributeMatch.Bool(resp.Match),
		fliptotel.AttributeValue.String(resp.VariantKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeReason.String(resp.Reason.String()),
		fliptotel.AttributeSegments.StringSlice(resp.SegmentKeys),
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagKey(resp.FlagKey),
		fliptotel.AttributeProviderName,
		fliptotel.AttributeFlagVariant(resp.VariantKey),
	}

	// add otel attributes to span
	span := trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)
	span.SetAttributes(spanAttrs...)

# Add Segment Match Type Field to Flipt Evaluation Responses

## Overview
Successfully implemented cross-language changes to add `segment_match_type` field to Flipt's evaluation response API. This field exposes whether evaluation matched a segment using ALL (AND) or ANY (OR) logic.

## Changes Made

### 1. Protobuf Schema (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto`)
Added new field to `VariantEvaluationResponse` message:
```protobuf
message VariantEvaluationResponse {
  bool match = 1;
  repeated string segment_keys = 2;
  EvaluationReason reason = 3;
  string variant_key = 4;
  string variant_attachment = 5;
  string request_id = 6;
  double request_duration_millis = 7;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp timestamp = 8;
  string flag_key = 9;
  string segment_match_type = 10;  // NEW FIELD
}
```

**Field Details:**
- **Type:** string
- **Tag Number:** 10 (next sequential tag after flag_key)
- **Values:**
  - "ALL" - All constraints in segment matched (AND operator)
  - "ANY" - At least one constraint matched (OR operator)
  - "" (empty) - No segment matched (e.g., threshold-based evaluation)

### 2. Generated Go Code (`rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go`)
Manually added struct field and getter method:

**Struct Field (Line 833):**
```go

    // ... existing fields ...

    SegmentMatchType      string                 `protobuf:"bytes,10,opt,name=segment_match_type,json=segmentMatchType,proto3" json:"segment_match_type,omitempty"`  // NEW
}
```

**Getter Method (Lines 931-936):**

```go
    }
```

### 3. Server Implementation (`internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`)

**Modified `variant()` Function:**
Updated to populate the segment_match_type field:
```go
if len(resp.SegmentKeys) > 0 {
    ver.SegmentKeys = resp.SegmentKeys
    // Determine segment match type based on which rule matched
    ver.SegmentMatchType = determineSegmentMatchType(ctx, flag, resp.SegmentKeys, s.logger)
}
```

**New Helper Function `determineSegmentMatchType()`:**
Implements logic to:
1. Iterate through flag rules to find matching rule
2. Match rule by comparing segment keys
3. Determine segment operator (AND → "ALL", OR → "ANY")
4. Return empty string if no segments matched

```go
func determineSegmentMatchType(ctx context.Context, flag *flipt.Flag, segmentKeys []string, logger *zap.Logger) string {
    if len(segmentKeys) == 0 {
        return ""
    }

    // Look for the rule that contains these segments
    for _, rule := range flag.Rules {
        ruleSegmentKeys := make(map[string]bool)
        for _, segment := range rule.Segments {
            ruleSegmentKeys[segment.Key] = true
        }

        // Check if this rule's segments match the evaluation's segments
        allSegmentsMatch := true
        for _, evalSegmentKey := range segmentKeys {
            if !ruleSegmentKeys[evalSegmentKey] {
                allSegmentsMatch = false
                break
            }
        }

        // Also check that the rule doesn't have extra segments
        if allSegmentsMatch && len(rule.Segments) == len(segmentKeys) {
            // Found the matching rule - determine operator
            switch rule.SegmentOperator {
            case flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
                return "ALL"
            case flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR:
                return "ANY"
            }
        }
    }

    return ""
}
```

## Implementation Details

### Segment Operator Mapping
- **flipt.SegmentOperator_AND_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (1)** → "ALL" - all constraints must match
- **flipt.SegmentOperator_OR_SEGMENT_OPERATOR (0)** → "ANY" - at least one constraint must match

### Evaluation Flow
1. `Variant()` function receives EvaluationRequest
2. Calls `s.evaluator.Evaluate()` which processes rules and returns matched segments
3. Calls new helper function with matched segment keys
4. Helper function finds matching rule and extracts segment operator
5. Populates `SegmentMatchType` field in response

### Batch Evaluation
Batch responses automatically include segment_match_type for each variant evaluation in the batch, as the response uses the same `VariantEvaluationResponse` type.

## Verification

✅ Proto schema syntax valid
✅ Generated Go code patterns follow protobuf conventions  
✅ Field tag numbers valid (no collisions)
✅ Getter methods match protobuf style
✅ Server implementation logic correct
✅ Operator mapping matches boolean evaluation logic
✅ Code formatting validated

## Files Modified

1. `/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.proto` - Proto schema
2. `/workspace/rpc/flipt/evaluation/evaluation.pb.go` - Generated Go code (8 lines added)
3. `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go` - Server implementation (~30 lines added)

## Testing Recommendations

1. **Unit Tests:** Test `determineSegmentMatchType()` with various rule/segment combinations
2. **Integration Tests:** Verify variant evaluation responses include correct segment_match_type values
3. **Edge Cases:** 
   - Multiple rules with same segments
   - Empty segment_keys
   - Threshold-based evaluations (should return empty string)

## Backward Compatibility

✅ Existing code continues to work
✅ JSON field name: `segment_match_type`
